The murderer was an illegal immigrant, gang-affiliated, and non-white; given this intersectionality, of course he couldn’t have known any better, for he was merely a victim of the white heteronormative system of Western patriarchal oppression he internalized upon economic migration into the United States. So this is a story with not one but two victims. The illegal immigrant didn’t kill Laken Riley; white people did.

This viewpoint is so repulsive it’s impossible to take seriously until you realize that this is literally what they believe—the bureaucrats and their activist allies who hold your legal, financial, and social fate in their hands.17 (Yes, an actual New York Times piece blames “White domination” for the “enduring and endemic violence” of non-whites. No, that’s not a misreading or misinterpretation.18) Hatred of the haves and adoration for the have-nots is not a bug in this system but its key feature. Normal people cannot believe it’s possible for unhumans to exist until they encounter them—until the microrevolution comes for them personally. Then it’s somebody should DO something but by then it’s too late. Terror has chosen you.

What also shocks normies is the brutality, the cruelty, the, uh, unfairness. Don’t these underprivileged groups simply want equality? Social justice? A hand up and a leg up? That all sounds good, to the cosmopolitan moderate. We live in a global community, after all, so can’t we all just get along? Imagine no countries, no religion, no possessions. Can’t the world just live as one?

Childish thinking betrays the fundamental misunderstanding of our situation that we brought up in Chapter 2—and of the season Western civilization is in. Consider that communist uprisings of the twentieth century and prior were conflicts of a legitimately aggrieved class against actual oppressors. Unhumans were able to amass eager followings for this very reason. But the United States has built the greatest system in world history for individual merit, social mobility, and universal education. Industrialization of Western Europe and then the US lifted the world out of feudalism and its rigid haves versus have-nots hierarchy. Then free markets (capitalism) could get to work lifting the rest of the developing world from poverty. This kicked in during the last half of the twentieth century. Without feudalism and social stagnation to fight, and with capitalism showing its superiority to lift people from poverty, the unhumans had to switch gears, literally, from manual laborers in factories and on farms as their chosen people to agitate, to other groups. This marked the great shift of Marxism from economics to sociology. Any group, class, caste, or other social identity that could (1) claim victimhood status and (2) identify a guilty party became a fertile environment for unhuman activity. They didn’t really have a choice. Communism had to swap out socioeconomic class struggle for other group differences because capitalism empowered so many have-nots to become haves. In the US, we don’t have a history of feudalism; we have a history of freedom that has been extended to more and more groups over time, meaning there are far fewer legitimate grievances here in the present than there are and have been abroad. This also means that communists can manufacture grievances to their dark little hearts’ content—just to make people mad and gain power over them. How do you deal with that?

For one, accept that this is our situation. Elon Musk put it this way:

Most reasonable people, because they are reasonable, cannot believe that the goal of the far left is to end America.19

You’ve come with us this far and so you now believe, or at the very least find the premise believable. Now comes the action. What to do about it.

Again, we cannot vote or shame our way out of a problem that neither of those got us into. So what does work? What crushes the communist? History leaves us with many questions but the occasional answer. This is one of them.

The Iron Law of Exact Reciprocity

Do you know what the longest, most-organized, and best-preserved legal text from the ancient world is? You might assume the laws of Moses in the Old Testament, perhaps the Ten Commandments specifically. Then you’d be wrong. Another set of laws predates the events of Exodus by three hundred years minimum: the Code of Hammurabi. The US Capitol displays a relief portrait of this Babylonian king for good reason, as his laws were the rule of his lands. From Hammurabi’s Code we get the very idea of “rule of law.” His were the first laws that human civilization recognized as essential to the establishment and existence of said civilization. From Hammurabi we also learn the most powerful persuasion technique that protects a society from those who would destroy it from within: reciprocity. Consider these excerpts from the Code:

Falsely accuse someone of murder, and you will be executed.

Receive a precious metal deposit to invest, and you must return it or its equivalent—even if you lose that original deposit.

Blind someone else, and you will be blinded.

Build a house not up to construction safety standards, and you will be made to correct the mistake at no cost to the customer.20

The Iron Law of Exact Reciprocity has been denigrated by well-meaning individuals over the centuries, with certain activists claiming that an eye for an eye makes the whole world blind. We laugh. This is obviously not the case. Eye-for-an-eye laws protect innocent eyes from assault by aspiring eye-gougers, who are now made to fear the consequence of that reciprocal eye removal law and rightly so. That’s reciprocity. Without reciprocity, we are without civilization. We become anti-civilization. We become: unhuman. This was true then, later, and now.

Do you know why the Cold War never turned kinetic? There were hot messes of misadventure to be sure, such as the ill-fated anti-guerrilla campaigns into communist Vietnam. Historians, filmmakers, and commentators have made careers out of their own pet answer to that question. Despite the proxy wars, the people of Earth never saw a nuclear war. We did not go extinct when we could have and perhaps nearly did. Why? The answer is as simple as it is primal. The State Department called it Atomic Diplomacy.21 We call it the state of humanity. Watch it play out in this totally real conversation that definitely took place in 30,000 BC.

Og: I have a big stick. Why shouldn’t I beat you to death with it and take your wife and cave?

Grog: Because I have a big stick, too. If you try to hit me with yours, I will beat you to death with mine first.

And so Og and Grog spoke softly and carried their big sticks. They lived out their days in peace. Descendants like Hammurabi would codify their finding into law. And that’s how all of us got here, with our inalienable rights to life, liberty, and property. Civilization cannot exist in the absence of reciprocity. Violence is nature’s way. We use it against her to shape, twist, crush, move, and otherwise manipulate her to our own devices, which, as humans, are to survive and to reproduce. The same goes in dealings with each other. Atomic Diplomacy is better known by its less-friendly descriptor: mutually assured destruction. The United States did not strike the Soviet Union with nuclear weapons because the Soviet Union would do the same in return, and vice versa.

To the principle of reciprocity, we’re now going to add the process for defeating communism. It is what the great men of history have done—and what their ideological allies across time could have done given the right resources—but reframed for our time.

c1AE

CHAPTER 13

THE PLAN: COUNTERREVOLUTIONARY STRATEGY AND TACTICS

I am firmly convinced that if, from the beginning of the revolutionary movement, Headquarters and the generals at the front had forgotten their personal interests and acted unanimously and resolutely, the Army would not have collapsed nor the interior fallen prey to anarchy, or at least things would have been checked in time.

—Pyotr Wrangel, Always with Honor

When the unhumans bring a show of force, team humanity must bring forth an even greater one. This is the only way.

So to fully map the process of crushing the Irregular Revolution, let’s briefly revisit the three defeats of communism from Chapter 4. Then we’ll see how successful communist crushers followed one or more of those paths to victory, with overwhelming might that brought the unhumans to well-earned ruin. And finally, we’ll seal the lesson with a call to action—how to fight and win the gray zone communist revolutionary war currently being waged in the United States. Let’s begin.

Three Ways to Crush the Revolution, Revisited

Communist revolutions have changed as warfare has changed. Welcome to the irregular revolution. Here’s how to defeat it.

1. The Ouroboros Option (The Snake Eats Itself)

Wherever unhumans emerge to feast on the flesh and blood of innocents, their unsatiated hunger and unquenched thirst subsequently drive them to eat each other. Those doing the doxxing and canceling will be doxxed and canceled by those more radical on their own team. Debankers, deplatformers, and otherwise destroyers of their enemies’ lifestyles and lives will then turn on their own. Already we have witnessed the radical left begin to eat its own, the great purge of #metoo being one notable example. Leftist-on-leftist gray-zone economic conflict, cyberwarfare, and lawfare, that mess was.

That said, this the first way to destroy anti-civilization is passive. It requires much time and great patience, which many of us may not have. Waiting it out is not ideal for those of us targeted for terror, for looting and killing in any way the unhumans can get away with (or get away from before getting caught and charged). We do not recommend re-creating the 1990s Russian depression, either for the United States as a whole—suffering an unprecedented and protracted national decline—or for us as canceled and humiliated individuals without independent stores of wealth and resources that can outlast 1990s Russia on American soil—which would be a world without supply chains, police, and in many cases electricity. We have not yet reached “peak woke” and in our view are nowhere near it. Previous communist seizures and purges have been thorough. The gray-zone revolutionary communists we face today are haphazard and prefer targets of convenience. This means they have covered much less ground, i.e., robbed and killed far fewer in meatspace, cyberspace, and all other spaces where irregular warfare is waged. The unhumans have their work cut out for them. They know this. They, like communist China with its one-hundred-year plan, are willing to wait out their prey. The predators will turn on each other, but we expect that final intraparty battle to take years if not decades.

What to do until they eat each other? Recall George Kennan’s containment strategy that prevented direct conflict with the Soviet Union and protected American allies and protectorates from Soviet influence and expansion. It worked. Scale the Kennan plan down from the national to the regional, local, and individual levels, and we might have a play here.

Containment requires keeping the unhumans where they are. Let them destroy themselves, yes, and far away from the rest of us. There shall be no footholds allowed in our territory, geographic, economic, or otherwise. We are free and will remain so. In the United States, that means state governors, county sheriffs, and district attorneys, you have the watch. It is up to you to contain evil where it is and stamp it out immediately and resolutely when and where it appears in your proximity. Reciprocity, remember? As for we the people, it is our job to support you financially and socially—particularly financially, for those of us with means.

Those of us who are unfortunately surrounded already, physically or socially or economically, we must get away. Like Wrangel’s White Army, retreat with honor. Assert your sovereign individualism—rebuild elsewhere, where it’s safe. This may mean a geographic move or an economic one for protection. Get your personal finances in order so you can afford to laugh at the cancel mobs when they come for your livelihood, make your income and investments independent of loyalty pledges demanded of you, and ensure the security of you and your loved ones.

The perfect situation is that communism is crushed before it must ever be contained. We will discuss how to defeat the uprising before it appears. But that may not be available for you, in the real world. You may already be a subject of unhumans. You are employed by unhumans. You are married to … you get it. You know. There’s nowhere for you to run or to hide. You are at the mercy of those who show no mercy. We will not fault you for doing what you must to survive, including taking the pledge through your lying teeth, hoping and praying that someone should just DO something. That’s what the next two ways to fight communism are. But be careful that while you suffer among the unhumans you don’t become one. Collaborators cannot regain a clean conscience.

This is why we do not advocate for waiting out the revolutionary war, with that one exception being the containment strategy. Now, the reason we’re a bit sour on letting the unhumans descend on one another to bring about their own defeat is it leaves the most vulnerable to their attack, well, vulnerable. Recall that the underclass communists prey on and persuade to do their bidding are oppressed worse after the revolution succeeds than after. They are led to their own slaughter and lied to the entire way. We have compassion for those who turn to anti-civilization. Many live unenviable lives and have nothing to live for—but the unhumans will give them something to kill and die for. This is not good. And so for the sake of all who will be targeted for microrevolutions now and later, we believe it prudent that we do not wait out Communist Revolution 2.0. Only the independently wealthy and location-independent have the freedom to do so, their fortunes protected by various offshoring strategies and with their livelihood decoupled from their reputation. In fact, they may have no reputation, remaining altogether anonymous and safe from unhuman harm. The risk for the revolution to come their way is already higher than for most given their likely designation as oppressors. Why should they who can save themselves stick their necks out? Consider the fate of Louis XIV; he thought himself and his family and fortune safe from the red terror engulfing his people. He could have chosen differently. So can some of you reading this book.

2. Great Men of Means

The great men and women of means, and history, usually did not view themselves as such. Those driven by ego and validation rarely make decisions that sacrifice both. Yet this is what the great ones must do. When the forces of anti-civilization have burned across a land, there have been a select few who saw what had to be done and had the will to do it—one strong man and his mates. Julius Caesar, Napoleon Bonaparte, Pyotr Wrangel, Francisco Franco, Chiang Kai-shek—each with their officers, their soldiers, their fighting men in arms. And those defensive firearms are needed given what has already transpired. When unhumans seize territory, first they ban guns. The unhumans then do what they will, and the unarmed innocent suffer what they must. Then along comes someone who doesn’t come along often. The one who utters in word or deed, as Franco did:

Wherever I am, there will be no communism.

And they mean it.

Historians choose who we remember. It is the great men of history who choose to be made memorable. Whenever such a man has willed communism into submission, it has always been with equitable means. The communist-socialists shoot the priests; Franco’s forces shoot them dead. Caesar’s enemies plotted to arrest him and establish their own new world order; Caesar arrested them first. Soviet sympathizers tried to poison the youth with media and schooling; Senator McCarthy poisoned their reputation to make them unemployable. Reciprocity.

This the second way to defeat the unhumans demands the means of reciprocation, which many of you reading this do not possess. It’s OK; you still get to support the one who does. You’ll know them when you see them, as they attract all the literal and metaphorical firepower of the enemy. Consider Elon Musk, the sole protector of anything like freedom of speech on the internet, who has been subjected to cruel and unusual lawfare by unhuman bureaucrats and activists. He must have our full support. Franco needed his generals; Bonaparte, his officers; Musk, his netizens.

That said, if you are one who could stay on the sidelines, sitting this one out to the end with your own family safe and your fortune intact, this might feel to you like a call to action. It is. You have the alignment, visibility, and at least some resources necessary to have a fighting chance at fighting back. You know this. You have the power. Do you have the will to use it?

Otherwise, your fate may be that of Louis XVI, in your own way and in your own time. You may go solemnly to the end and everything you love with you, deceived by a false sense of safe escape. It didn’t have to go that way. You had an opening. Opportunity. Power. But not will.

Have the will to power. And if you do, here’s how you can use it.

Great Deeds for Great Men and the Iron Law of Exact Reciprocity

We’ll get right to it. The great American counterrevolution to depose the Cultural Marxists must occur on all terrains of society they currently possess and on those they aim to seize. This is tantamount to total victory. It is achievable but only with the resolve of Franco and the thoroughness of McCarthy.

Cultural Marxists run operations in media, government, education, economy, family, religion, and arts and entertainment. This is what they do; this is what they’ve done, having completed a long march through the institutions. As a result, and as only a few examples, targeted lawfare to take down private citizens and political enemies is succeeding, as they hold key prosecutorial and judicial positions. Schools are littered with anti-American propaganda to train up a new Red Guard; meanwhile, children deemed members of the oppressor race and religion are punished and persecuted by both administration and classmates and those of the alleged oppressed race are given passing grades for failing class and actual passes for violent behavior. Cultural Marxists have also infiltrated mainline Protestant Christian denominations to recast Jesus Christ from spiritual messiah to socioeconomic radical who wants to raise your taxes. (If while reading that you thought, What lawfare? What propaganda? What churches? then we really can’t help you. Greatness demands minimum viable awareness of what’s going on. Some reading this lack it. There may still be a place for you supporting those leading the counterrevolution.)

What else can be done to turn the tide? Let’s let reciprocity answer the question, specifically, the Iron Law of Exact Reciprocity. Eyefor-an-eye protects innocent eyes from future assault. So this is what the great men of our time can do:

A humiliation tactic—naming and shaming—most famously used in Mao’s China can be repurposed to beat the Cultural Marxists at their own game. Terror is a double-edged weapon.

What we need are lists. Turning Point USA publishes a “Professor Watchlist” with dossiers on college and university staff known to “discriminate against conservative students, promote anti-American values and advance leftist propaganda in the classroom.”1 They hate this. Good. This is a start, so let’s keep going, and with better-funded publicity. We should all know their names for their shame. McCarthy made beloved Americans total industry outcasts in an instant with exposés of their secret subversive activities. We need men and women of action to do the same—and to fund it. Yes in education but also in media, throughout the economy, and more. This could take the form of well-documented (and well-promoted) lists with dossiers, or it could be more highly targeted. When Elon Musk purchased Twitter, he labeled National Public Radio as “US state-affiliated media” and later “Government Funded Media.” NPR, known for consistently misrepresenting news through that oppressor-oppressed lens, thrashed at the charge. Upward of 11 percent of NPR’s budget comes from direct and indirect government funding.2 NPR rage-quit Twitter as a result and has not returned. Musk’s micro-counterrevolutionary effort succeeded.

And yet this amounts to perhaps 0.01 percent of the effort required to identify and oust Cultural Marxists from positions and institutions in their clutches. Reciprocity will continue to guide us. Whichever organizations and influencers across the social terrain are engaging in microrevolution against normal people, put them on the list. Then, publish that list. Then promote it. Advertise the counterrevolution. Let Cultural Marxists tremble in fear that they will be named and shamed, just as they have named and shamed so many into ruin. Reciprocity works. It’s mutually assured cancellation. The unhumans will not stop until they are stopped.

The needle has moved a little in this effort. Consider the work of Christopher Rufo and James O’Keefe. Rufo is known for unveiling the serial plagiarism that brought down former Harvard University president Claudine Gay, a notable DEI hire (in this context, DEI meaning “Didn’t Earn It”). Rufo is despised by the unhumans because he uses their own weapon against them to great effect. Another similar counterrevolutionary strategist is Chaya Raichik, creator of Libs of TikTok, whose standard operation is simply reposting radicals’ own subversive social media content for a broader audience to see (and be horrified by).

Now, as for O’Keefe, he has for years exposed minions of the forces of unhumanity in government, media, and economic mainstays such as healthcare. His infiltrative work reveals all manner of office politics, infighting, and gossip, yes, but also leaves naked the extent to which giant organizations have been intentionally hollowed out by unhuman efforts. Unfortunately, we haven’t witnessed much change afterward. The minion staffer deletes their social media after O’Keefe goes public, leftist media publishes hit pieces about O’Keefe, O’Keefe gains support for more work, and on the cycle goes. What we need are 1,001 more special operators like O’Keefe, Raichik, and Rufo— and men of great means backing them. Also necessary is something like a step-by-step process for maximizing the counterrevolutionary effectiveness of their infiltrative and revelatory work. In O’Keefe’s case, the unhumans in control are the ones the public needs to see on hidden cameras. That footage must then be entered into the record as evidence, with reciprocal lawfare waged against these individuals until they are ousted in shame and their organizations brought to heel. We have yet to see statesmen demonstrate a will to do so. That must change.

Reciprocal lawfare must be a response to the lawfare experienced now in the United States and the Collective West. There will be no stopping of it until this occurs. Consider the power of a legal subpoena. These cost organizations thousands of dollars in legal bills just to respond to, not to mention the vast amounts of time required. Attorney generals in red districts could easily be going after Antifa, BLM or the array of Soros-affiliated NGOs. RICO lawsuits could easily be brought as well. One obvious example would be in the realm of NGOs that profit from illegal immigration, via taxpayer dollars. Why hasn’t the AG of Texas cracked down on them? Alabama? Mississippi? The list goes on. If no reciprocity is felt, they will keep reaching further and further with their lawfare, including the leftist judges on the bench. The only answer to this is exact reciprocity. We’ll see if Republicans have the stomach for it.

Organized boycotts are another tool for cultural counterrevolution. They work, as witnessed in 2023 with the influencer-led boycott of Bud Light products. The beermaker lost a projected $1 billion in sales.3 Alas, revenue has begun to recover, as many conservative Americans targeted by company marketing have returned to purchasing it. Blame our country’s cultural alcoholism, yes, but also recognize that power requires will to maintain. The longer boycotts last, the better they work.

“But that’s, like, totally not nice,” some principled conservatives have said of boycotts. Understand the time and the season. Gray zone revolution is not occurring in a vacuum or in a state with no prior history. A civilization built on law and order demands the maintenance of that law and order or soon there is no civilization left. There is a reason convicted criminals are punished (or used to be). Restitution is reciprocity. It’s Hammurabi. We forget this to our own shame and to those who will be targeted by the unhumans we could have stopped. Nothing here in this section or in this book advocates illegal violence. Nothing. We do advocate for legal weapons of mass persuasion. The enemies of truth and justice are already using them, and our recourse is to use them back. If that’s shame, use shame. If that’s money, use money.

Speaking of money, why does NPR receive 11 percent of their budget from federal, state, and local governments? Why? Could it be that taxpayers do not realize they are funding Cultural Marxism directly? And could it be that if they were informed by mass awareness campaigns that they would choose for their hard-earned money to be spent elsewhere? Could it?

Which brings us to our biggest ask of all. Those of you reading this book with influence in the federal government, this is for you:

The time is right and technology available to propose and pass a National Tax Transparency Act. This new law, duly enacted following valid and corrective legislative and executive procedure, will allow for the permanent visibility of the citizenry as to the spending of their federal taxes down to the last dollar. It is no secret unhumans have parasitized the national governments of many Western countries, funneling the public treasury back into their minions’ pockets through various media, education, economic, religious, and art and entertainment initiatives and groups whose explicit objective is to demolish Western civilization. Our ask is not even that this be made to stop; it’s that the man or woman who understands what our moment calls for put forward the action plan to allow all America to know this is occurring.

This mirrors the list tactic. To be forced into the open is to let your covert manipulation lose its advantage. So let the people see. Let the people trace every tax return, every estimated payment, every withheld-from-the-paycheck dollar to its final destination. Then let the public decide how they feel about it—and how they feel about those allocating the budget. Care can be taken to protect classified materials and projects, of course. But that same culture of bureaucratic secrecy that built a taxpayer panopticon is the very problem—the federal government demands total transparency into how we earn our money so they can tax it, while we have absolute-zero visibility into how that taxed money is spent.

On the topic of visibility, the National Tax Transparency Act could be paired with other legislation mandating transparency into voting systems at the federal, state, and local levels. Advances in technology now allow for security and privacy so every voter could look up every vote they cast after the fact to confirm no one else voted in their name, their vote was not counted more than once, and indeed their vote was in fact counted. Cryptography, blockchain, and other decentralized tools such as Zero-Knowledge Proofs are able to put this idea into action, all of it with existing tech. Of course, the days of representative democracy are themselves numbered, as The Sovereign Individual predicted; in the digital age it no longer makes sense for citizens to have decisions made on their behalf and especially not by those manipulated by lobbying, blackmail, and other interests opposed to the citizens’ welfare. We see a day coming when every citizen is a democracy unto themselves as well as a budget allocator; what laws they desire to abide by, they will pass for themselves. What projects they wish to fund, they will self-allocate money toward. This is the future of government, perhaps the far future, but the future nonetheless. And transparency into both taxation and voting results are the great transitional form between the present and this glorious future where sovereign individuals may live free.

We have a way to go. Returning to the present, we realize that advanced privacy tools could maintain one-way privacy so only you know how you voted and not some unelected DEI bureaucrat-activist. We believe that voting transparency and “trust but verify” records are a transitional form to the ultimate state of democracy, which is that each citizen is a lawgiver unto him or herself. In a digital world where information is nearly free to transmit and consume, it does not make logical (or technological) sense for someone else to make laws on your behalf while you have no say, hide those laws in omnibus bills, or levy and spend your tax money in any way you deem unfit. In a post-revolutionary future when Team Humans have won, we foresee that when you disagree with a given law then, as a law-abiding citizen, you will not have to comply with it. And if you do not want your tax dollars funding an activity you disagree with, you will be able to opt out and either save that money or devote it into a more productive activity.

The best way to defeat the irregular revolution we’re facing is to stop funding it. The second-best way is to deplete it of revolutionaries. Just as the great men of history target the subversives to neutralize their behavior, we must not forget their potential followers who would do their bidding, led on by a promise of fortune and glory if only they cast aside all sense of humanity and commit unspeakable atrocity. In former times, our elite were endowed with noblesse oblige, which was the recognition that with high status came high responsibility, specifically for the disadvantaged and downtrodden, those various groups who left to their lot in life make ideal targets for perversion into the forces of unhumanity. This is what was forgotten in the various empires that fell to the communist revolution. We forgot at our own peril.

Modern noblesse oblige in the US requires great men and women of equal will and power in waging effective gray-zone war, now in a different way. What gives the underclass hope is a way up from it—a path to success. It is not possible to have hope when anarcho-tyrants reign, forcing the poorest to suffer the most at the hands of lawlessness, as they are least able to afford to leave or find alternative employment if their barely stable situation is upended, as happened to millions in the 1960s and in 2020. Numerous ills plague the underclass, from single parenthood to drug abuses to perpetual poverty. Hollowing out of Rust Belt careers from the 1970s through the 1990s due to lower-paid labor arbitrage in China brought ruin upon millions of former proud working-class Americans. We expect the Artificial Intelligence Revolution to eliminate the careers of those who somehow escaped globalization.

Historically, left-wing activists have claimed to care for the least of these most. And we do need the compassionate liberal—but we need to give them a better system than merely the goal of “helping” with zero-accountability government dollars that do more harm than any good as discussed in Chapter 9. Consider the life and work of John H. Patterson, the turn-of-the-century entrepreneur and philanthropist who made worker welfare as high a priority as profit. He introduced cleaner conditions, safer machinery, higher wages, and better hours to the workforce of National Cash Register, together with no-cost meal and entertainment opportunities. At first these measures were criticized by fellow capitalists as extreme and unnecessary, but the Daytonian’s outsized success persuaded the American industrial elite to treat their employees like human beings. Patterson’s compassionate capitalist is likely why the United States did not suffer a “hot” communist revolution in the same period as Russia, Spain, China, and others; the American underclass had a ladder handed down to them so they could climb their way up into stable working-class and even middle-class prosperity. Unfortunately, from the 1970s onward, our elite have kicked the ladder down. They imperil themselves.

What then is to be done by our modern-day John Pattersons who have the means to rescue the have-nots of America from socioeconomic destitution and other paths to resentment? Consider:

Privately funded, local, and small, intimate programs that teach a systems approach to creating success in your personal life, from parenting peacefully to personal budgeting, have the potential to raise multiple generations out of poverty and into stability, for generations to come. There is only the question of who will fund and run them; would-be megadonors, we ask that you prioritize the salvation of your civilization above and beyond your portfolio’s performance next quarter. Volunteers are needed, both to protect people from joining the revolution and to save them from its destruction. The revolution eats its own. We wish to save our countrymen and women from this fate.

Furthermore, to raise the downtrodden up from cyclical poverty and into prosperity, we recommend the immediate banning of all public education unions in the United States, as these institutions hold a near-monopoly on the rearing of America’s publicly schooled children and are thus uniquely responsible for the disparity in outcomes between and among underclass, working, middle, and upper-class students. They’ve got to go. They already know better, as the most vocal proponents of teachers’ unions in America send their children to private school. So let free-market competition drive citizens to the best education solutions for their children, be that public, private, home, or otherwise. A full-scale lawfare assault against the teachers’ unions until every last one is shut down is a necessary path forward. We ask for no violence—only reciprocity. Add to that the forfeiture of all universities and colleges that have received taxpayer funding. Higher education as an institution has failed to prepare the next generation of the workforce to rebuild our infrastructure and create the future and instead have burdened millions with debt that is inescapable even from bankruptcy. Sometimes complex problems demand simple solutions. The student loan debt in the US is $1.73 trillion, and the total endowment of all US colleges and universities is a market value of $927 billion.4, 5 The latter will cover just about half of the former. For the rest, student loan debt will be made dischargeable in bankruptcy. Each loan payee will see their debt nearly halved. For recouping the rest, should they so choose, loan holders will be permitted to receive a refund for any tuition paid for which they received an education they are unsatisfied with, e.g., a degree that failed to prepare them for gainful employment. The refund amount would not exceed the total remaining balance of loans due.

To be clear, this is a population that could easily be wielded and mobilized by a BLM Chavez-type figure. Trust me, you do not want to wait around for that figure to emerge.

For future higher education affordability, we agree with this recommendation from renowned psychology professor and researcher Geoffrey Miller:

The real way to ‘make college more affordable’, insofar as college degrees function mostly as proxies for general intelligence for employment purposes, is for the Supreme Court to overturn Griggs v. Duke Power Co (1971) & allow employers to use cheap, fast, reliable, valid IQ tests for hiring, instead of college degrees.6

Every problem the gray-zone irregular communist revolution has thrust on America has an obvious solution. We have presented a few essentials here for consideration of the great men and future great of history inspired by this book. Surely there are superior versions of these ideas and others altogether we had not considered. Regardless, great men of action will be needed.

All this will take the will to power, with that power being for the benefit of people. Within one calendar year, we foresee all student loan debt eliminated and university corruption ended, with only those higher education opportunities that serve their students and prepare them for productive careers surviving this necessary transformation. A secondary result would be a baby boom so great that the population decline problem will resolve itself within the decade if not half-decade. The future is bright only if we make it so.

Naturally, the unhumans will not be happy with these efforts and especially not with those heading them. They will fight back. For everything they’ve got. Dragons don’t like it when the gold they’ve looted is returned. So we must fight back harder, with more resolve in our hearts than resentment in theirs. We will follow the leader. But in each domain—education, government, and so on—history demands more than one leader. Otherwise, it is all for naught. Consider this a word of warning, aspiring great men of history reading this book:

The honor and courage of Wrangel, Chiang, and others defeated by unhuman forces deserved better. We can’t change their past but we can redirect our future. Victory over evil never comes down to one man in the arena. This is romantic but a fantasy. Recall the words of Wrangel as they opened this chapter: “unanimous and resolute.” Any strategy or tactic deployed to crush the unhumans that is not both unanimous and resolute will fail.

Any insights we’ve gleaned from the secret history of communist revolutions are worthless if attempts to put them into practice are done scattershotly by separate individuals and isolated organizations each pursuing their own ends with their own unique means, all without coordinated timing. So while we praise Musk, we realize he is in a precarious position, in need of an elite peer group of generals and a metaphorical infantry to come to his aid.

The great man always needs an army. The network swarm targets individuals and institutions deemed vulnerable. So only individuals and institutions more powerful than the swarm can defeat it, can send it back to the hell from whence it came. That might be you and yours.

You’ll know.

3. Victory before Battle

Reciprocity. It is possible to bring a society to ruin without warfare, to conquer it by dividing it. So, too, are there means to crush the uprising before it gets into stance. The gray zone communist war for America has already begun, but there will be millions more battles. Every day there are skirmishes. Spats. Squads of unhumans besieging their unsuspecting targets. We know what they’re going to do. They’re going to incite, seize, and purge, same as they’ve always done, but quietly this time around, targeting good, honest people one by one. These are the patriots we see in trending news daily—another one sentenced to prison, another one bankrupted from lawfare, another one ousted from their successful career, another one dead from an alleged suicide (it wasn’t). No more. We know what the unhumans are going to do. So we can do it, too—we can win before fighting.

Team humanity can also prepare the environment of battles for our purpose, which is total victory. We can separate. We can message. We can infiltrate. And we must. Waiting it out is not an option for all of us, and it is not the best first choice for any of us. Meanwhile, we do admit that except for a few shining knights whose armor takes the arrows, there do not seem to be enough great men in the public eye or private sphere to protect all that Western civilization has to offer future generations, at least not yet. Unhumans are soiling and burning as much of it as they can, at the institutional level and the individual. A guy who builds rockets and buys Twitter back from an unhuman regime is a lot but not nearly enough. We have throughout this book pilloried the old right wing—those politicians, pundit caste, and philanthropists whose absence on the battlefield is noticeable every day in every way, each time another vulnerable target is taken. Conservatives, moderates, and others who do have the means to put up a powerful public fit are pulling a Louis XVI. As X account @wokal_distance wrote:

Left Wing Billionaires think like great men of history whose goal is to change the world. Right Wing Billionaires think middle managers whose goal is to not go broke. That’s why the left invests in things that change society, while [the] right only invests in things that make money.7

For what shall it profit a man if he gains the whole world but loses his own civilization?

And so until such a time as new American Caesars, Wrangels, Francos, Chiangs, or McCarthys reveal themselves, it’s probably up to us. To you, your family and friends, your network. Your “people.” And any VIPs you know, in whatever station of society they’re in.

That said, we must admit that we’ve struggled writing this section, on how the third way to defeat the unhumans applies to our present day. This is because historical precedent is slim. There is of course the Tank Man, a noble symbol of losing on principle. There has not yet been Tank Men—a force of united normal people so vast in number, so mighty in resolve, that the enemy never stood a chance despite otherwise superior firepower and institutional backing.

There was the Caesar who crossed the Rubicon, who crushed what could have become a proto-communist uprising. But this was the great man of history, nipping rebellion in the bud. Other revolts in other times and places such as those in nineteenth-century France were put down, again by military leaders with better-than-reciprocal resources to fight the forces of unhumanity.

They say communism has never been tried. This is false. But what is true is that defeating communist has never been tried by normal people. By people like you and us. We can nip this thing in the bud. But it’s going to require yet another paradigm shift. The first new frame we’ve asked you to adopt is that the United States is likely in the throes of a gray-zone communist revolutionary war. The signs are present and the evidence accessible, with odds (much) higher than 10 percent that our dark hypothesis is correct.

In gray zone warfare, there is no distinction between civilian and combatant. You know this in theory. And now, we are asking you to accept it in practice. We are asking you to become a combatant. Because you already are.

How Normal People Can Crush Communist Revolution 2.0

Everything we have said in this book will be twisted out of context by our unhuman enemies. This is what they do. They will of course leave out the part we’ll say next. We will say it anyway because it is the right thing to do.

Unhumans rob and kill. We do not.

Illegal and harmful acts to further any political cause should be condemned totally. We do. Thus, all commentary of ours should be interpreted in the spirit of law and order. We cannot save civilization by suspending it. That is what the unhumans do; they promise a better world on the other side of a far, far worse one. They lie. They guarantee easy heaven and deliver perpetual hell.

We suggest you do what it takes to win before the fight. To protect yourself, your family, your city, your state, and your country from the unhuman battles to come. We are asking you to unite with others of like mind and spirit. And together, we will crush the communist revolution.

Here’s how we the people are going to do it.

Counterrevolutionary OPE to Win

What they do to us, we do right back. In the case of counterrevolutionary warfare, we must all shore ourselves up so that we can defend ourselves in the event we are targeted for microrevolution, when the anonymous hordes of social media or the HR department attempt to incite, seize, and purge. We will be ready. This is war. An irregular war, yes. But a war. Now we will act like it.

And so we will follow OPE Stage 1, Separate. For normal people, that means building a network of like-minded people you can trust. Remember the terrains of society: government, media, education, economic, religious, and art and entertainment. Which of these pertain to your life? Your local government officials from the school board and sheriff deputies to district attorney, prosecutor, the chief of police. Who actively does the work of safeguarding law and order around you? These are your people. Know them by name, and they, you. The same goes for media you consume. Separate yourself from people who hate your values and support independent creators who honor and valorize them. Do all business you can this way, working with and buying from those who are values aligned and shunning your dollar from those who launder their profits into subversive activity. This ought not need to be said and yet it does. Consider also the education of your children if you have any. Is it best to allow them to be propagandized by radicals who despise Western civilization and everything our heritage has entrusted us with? If not, bring them home to homeschool or unschool, or consider an independent values-aligned religious school. Start your teenagers at a centrist community college, not a lifetime-of-debt major university where they are at risk of getting turned into actual communists. Consider alternative income sources besides an 8-to-5 job so you can hold your head high if you are asked to recant a belief everyone on the American left held ten years ago. Buy your free speech rights back with a side hustle or self-employment opportunity. These opportunities are not difficult to find if you have the will to look.

You must prepare your environment for counteroperation so if and when the microrevolution comes to you, your family, or your community, you will have set apart your allies and your resources. They’ll have your back. You will be ready.

OPE Stage 2, Message, can occur simultaneously with the first. Or after. Or way after. Or way before. Or when the microrevolt against you is already at hand. Warfare in the gray zone is irregular, messy, chaotic, out of order sometimes. So can the preparation of your environment for it be, at times. This may be one of them.

The only message you will need to protect your loved ones from revolutionary persuasion and also neutralize those who do ever come for you is the one message that no unhuman has ever been able to withstand. It is their first and last kryptonite. It is the unhuman’s bane: laughter.

So mock the unhumans. Humiliate the unhumans. Ridicule the unhumans. Disgrace, debase, and deride the unhumans. Put the unhumans to shame. Tease and taunt and parody the unhumans. Scorn, scoff, and sneer.

If this is what you’ll do when the unhumans attempt a microuprising against you, why are we talking about it in Operational Preparation of the Environment for counterrevolution? Two reasons. One, this is a decision you make ahead of time, not in the moment. Cancel mobs and serial doxxers force their targets into submission through unforeseen terror. There was just no way this tax-paying, rule-following ’merican could ever deserve such treatment. Then came the unhumans to steal and kill and destroy. Lives broken and shattered. This is what they do.

And so now is the time to decide you will deploy the unhuman’s bane at first chance and upon first glance from the unhumans. You will not attempt to turn the tables on their feelings with your facts. This is why conservatives, moderates, and garden-variety liberals lose. You cannot reason with that which rejects reason. Resentment is their logic; envy, their thinking. You are a decided oppressor and thus deserving of the worst treatment they can muster in this low-intensity conflict context.

So decide now. That you will be like former President Donald Trump commenting on the 2024 State of the Union address delivered by President Joe Biden. President Trump did not critique or fact-check or call out the various logical fallacies Biden deployed by name. No, he used Snapchat filters to give President Biden and Vice President Kamala Harris goofy faces. He took them as seriously as he believed they deserved to be taken.

Also at the time of this writing, in the news was social commentator and cartoonist Stonetoss, who was doxxed by self-proclaimed communists online. The artist behind the comic had all the usual accusations foisted upon him. What did he do? Did he react with fear, tremble in terror, publish an apology letter written in legalese, and shut down his accounts? This is exactly what many public figures and private individuals have done, so what did Stonetoss do?

His first post after the doxxing was to announce a special sale on his cartoon tie-in plush toy. Subsequent posts of this used creative memes, GIFs, and other media to mock his accusers, promote the sale, and prove his mettle. The sale was so popular and volume of orders so high, customers reportedly crashed his ecommerce store.8 Haters are your most valuable marketers.

You may not have a product to sell, but you probably have a reputation to protect. So when the mob comes to seize your dignity and purge your good name, ruin theirs first—with laughter. Neutralize the terror. Turn around, point at the big, dark monster lurching toward you in the hallway, and laugh. As in dreams, so in reality.

The message our laughter sends is twofold—you’re telling the mob, in effect, Where I am, there will be no communism, in your own way. And you’re also spreading a message of hope to other potential targets, setting the example for those in your circle and those who later hear about what happened—how you withstood the mob with a smile and maybe made some money off their hate-promoting you. You disarm the mob not just for yourself but for other like-minded people in your environment. Which is the second reason why we’ve placed this in counterrevolutionary OPE. When you’ve built a network of influencers, you can call on them to aid you in your time of need. Returning fire with persuasion will not be you against the mob; it will be you and your generals and officers, your colleagues and key connections, giving the mob a twist of their own tool.

One more thing: Never apologize. Ever. You will not express remorse. You will not explain yourself. You will not “add context.” This is your life; the unhumans come to destroy it. Imagine saying you’re sorry to them. Couldn’t be us.

This transitions us right into OPE Stage 3, Infiltrate, and we find ourselves coming full circle. Recall the terrains of society that in OPE Stage 1 we said pertain to you, as well as the relationships you will have strategically built within them—in government, in education, in media, for example. There are the people you need to know, whose support you may need and camaraderie you may share, yes. Now who needs to know you? Where do you fit? What local government race could you enter? What homeschool co-op could you lead? What after-school program for the neighborhood kids could you start? What side business could you build with like-minded people?

You may not consider yourself a great hero of history, but we need great people in local positions of influence. Your local parks department, library system, and school board are all institutions that subversives infiltrate if the opportunity presents itself. Volunteering may not make a lot of money, but it makes an eternal difference. Think beyond the bottom line; civilization depends on each of us doing what we can, be that serving on a parks or library board or committee or running in a local election.

OPE Stage 3 of the counterrevolution may require actual infiltration of existing institutions. Alternatively, if institutions with influence over you are too corrupted or too incompetent to be salvaged even from within, then building your own decentralized alternative may be the best way, as with the examples of homeschool leadership in your community or entrepreneurship, building a company of consequence in an industry overrun by Cultural Marxists with few non-woke choices.

This OPE Stage serves the other two and is in turn served by them. Effective preparation means you and yours will be safe. The microrevolution should it come will look to you pitiable, not terrible. You will laugh them off, even reverse-cancel anyone who attempts to do the same to you. You can also borrow tactics from the second way to defeat communism, where you perhaps organize a counter-boycott set against you, or collect signatures to recall an unhuman-sympathizer from a critical public office as punishment for their neglect of (or protection of) any anarcho-tyranny near you.

You may not be destined to become the great men of history. But you can be a good one. For yourself, your family, and your civilization. And if we have millions of people who do that, we can undo what the unhumans have already done in America. Our efforts may take twenty to forty years. It will be worth it. Because …

We Are Going to Win

Yes, it is possible to defeat the unhumans. We can keep any and all would-be subversives terrified of acting on their impulses with full knowledge of what will happen to them if they try. If there is anything you set to your long-term memory from this book, it is this: The unhumans will not stop unless they are stopped. And they can be.

Please remember what you have read in this book and more importantly how you have felt while reading it. We will leave you with these words of Francisco Franco:

I say this to you because we Spaniards are a forgetful people, because we are used to living for the moment, because we do not look back, because we do not know how to see the chain of heroes, because we do not contemplate the sum of sacrifices.9

The communist revolution is the darkest chapter in human history. For whatever reason, perhaps by divine providence, it has come to us to end that chapter once and for all.

We will.

We’re going to win.

c1DT

Every book has a backstory. We would like to thank a few special people behind this one. Thank you to Blake Neff, Jack Posobiec’s cohost for the Human Events Daily series Chronicles of the Revolution that initially inspired this book. And thank you Angelo Fazio and Russ Spacy, the series producers for that as well as The China Files. And finally, thank you, Cynthia Yockey: You supported this project with thorough research; your work was indispensable and invaluable.

c1NW

ABOUT THE AUTHORS

Jack Posobiec is senior editor at Human Events and host of Human Events Daily, which has more than 250 million downloads. He is a veteran U.S. Navy intelligence officer with deployments to Guantanamo Bay and East Asia. Posobiec’s final deployment was as intelligence director for Navy Expeditionary Forces Command Pacific—Task Force 75. Posobiec has authored three books: Citizens for Trump: The Inside Story of the People’s Movement to Take Back America, 4D Warfare: A Doctrine for a New Era of Political Warfare, and The Antifa: Stories from Inside the Black Bloc. In 2019, Posobiec was awarded a Lincoln Fellowship by the Claremont Institute. A Temple University—Philadelphia, graduate, Posobiec lived in China before settling in Washington, DC, with his wife and two sons.

Joshua Lisec writes books of consequence. He is a Wall Street Journal bestselling ghostwriter with more than eighty books ghostwritten that have been translated into a dozen languages. Lisec is best known for his literary collaborations with controversial public figures, capturing their authentic voice and conveying the whole story. Lisec is also the author of the bestselling irreverent guide to entrepreneurship So Good They Call You a Fake and creator of The Best Way to Say It® writing programs. In 2021, he was executive producer of Better Left Unsaid, an award-winning documentary exposing the suppressed history of communist uprisings. Joshua has been featured in Publishers Weekly, Newsweek, Forbes, BBC, TEDx, Sky News, and TMZ, among others. Joshua lives with his wife and children near Dayton, Ohio.
